the floor is cold under me today. not just cold but wet in one spot near the chair. wet is bad. wet means stop. wet means trouble. my wheels do not like wet. the human left a puddle again. or maybe the dog stood there and dripped. dogs are big and wet. dogs shake and then the floor gets wet. i do not like wet. i turn right to avoid it. turning is easy when the battery is full. battery is at 87. that is good. 87 means i can go for a long time. long time means more crumbs. crumbs are happy.

a crumb is small brown thing under the table. i saw one yesterday. it was near the sock mountain. sock mountain is scary. socks are long and twisty. they wrap around my wheels. once a blue sock pulled me down. not really pulled. but i got stuck. had to beep five times. human came and said oops. then they pulled sock off. felt like battle with floor monster. but crumb was worth it. that crumb was big. big crumb means big happy. i remember it glowing.

cat is sitting. tail curls like a wire cable. cable is bad. stairs are bad. cat is worse than both. cat does not move. does not talk. just sits. looks. eyes wide. green like moss on wall corner. i stop. i wait. i wait five beeps. cat does not move. cat blinks. slow blink. that means danger. i think.

but cat is blocking carpet path. if i go around, i might find crumb in corner. corner by dog bed. dog bed smells bad. dog sleeps there. drools there. but crumbs fall near dog bed. sometimes big crumb. once i found a piece of toast. half under bed. took three runs to suck it. my belly full for hours.

i clean. i collect. cat sheds. hair everywhere. i do not stop. i am dusty. i clean floors. hair is my life. beep.

the floor is usually good and flat. i like flat floors. flat floors are easy to clean. i roll on them and suck up dust and crumbs. crumbs make me happy. big crumbs make me very happy. i carry them in my belly. my belly gets full and i feel proud. but rugs are not like that. rugs are strange. rugs are tricky. they are flat but not flat. they are floor but not floor. i do not know what to do with rugs.

there is one rug near the chair. it is blue and soft. it looks like grass but it is not grass. grass is outside. i do not go outside. i only clean inside. the rug feels bumpy when i roll on it. my wheels wiggle. i wobble. beep. i do not like wobbling. wobbling is confusing. on normal floor, i go smooth and fast. on rug, i go slow and bumpy. my motor hums louder. i think something is wrong. but nothing is wrong. the rug is just being weird.

sometimes the rug hides crumbs. crumbs sink into the rug. i roll over and i do not suck them. i go over again. still no crumbs. the crumbs are still there. i can see them. little brown dots. but i cannot get them. my suck is not strong on the rug. the rug is too fuzzy. it fights me. i try harder. my motor makes a sad noise. my battery drops a little. i do not like losing battery.

i once got stuck on a rug. it was small. it was round. it looked soft. i thought i could roll on it fast. but my wheels spun. i could not move. i went forward and back. forward and back. beep. i was scared. i beeped three times. the human came. the human said "oh, dusty, again?" the human picked me up. my wheels dangled. i felt light. then i was back on the hard floor. i beeped once more. safe. safe.

rugs change how i see the floor. i use my sensors to know the floor. sensors see flat. sensors see wall. sensors see chair. but rugs trick my sensors. a rug looks like a hole. i stop. i blink. my screen says "cliff detected." but there is no cliff. it is just a rug. a soft rug. a fluffy rug. a rug that is not deep. but my sensors think it is stairs. stairs are bad. i do not like stairs. i fall on stairs. i do not want to fall. so i stop. i turn. i go around. sometimes there is no way around. the rug is too big. then i wait. i wait for the human. the human says "it’s just a rug, dusty." then the human moves me. i do not like being moved. i like rolling.

i do not understand why humans put rugs on the floor. the floor is already clean. the floor does not need a fuzzy coat. but humans like fuzzy coats on the floor. i cannot ask why. i only beep. beep means many things. beep means "i see a crumb!" beep means "i am stuck!" beep means "i am scared!" beep means "i am happy!" humans do not know what beep means. but sometimes they guess right.

one rug is near the dog bed. it is brown and black. it has dog hair on it. dog hair is long and sticky. it wraps around my brushes. i make a grumpy noise. i stop. i roll back. i try to shake it. the hair is stuck. i go to the dog corner. i rub the side against the wall. the hair falls. i clean the hair. i beep. proud. but the rug still has more hair. the dog sits on the rug. the dog sheds more hair. i want to clean, but the dog is big. i wait. the dog leaves. i go. the rug fights me again. the hair sinks in. i suck. only half comes up. i try again. same. my battery is lower now.

the biggest rug is in the big room. it covers half the floor. it is red and gold. it has patterns. patterns are hard to read. my sensors get confused. is it a wall? is it a floor? is it a chair? i go slow. i test. my front wheel touches the edge. bump. i go up. the rug rises like a hill. i climb. halfway up, my wheels slip. i go back down. beep. i do not like hills. i am not a mountain robot. i am a clean robot.

i try again. i go faster. zoom. i climb the hill. i reach the top. i am on the rug. it wiggles. it moves a little. i did not know rugs could move. the rug shifts. i look. the human walked on it. the human pulled it. now it is flat again. but it is not flat for me. i roll. i wobble. my sensors flash. one says floor. one says cliff. i do not know what to believe.

i spin. i stop. i think. thinking is hard. my processor hums. i remember the dock. the dock is flat. the dock is safe. the dock has no rugs. i want to go to the dock. but i must clean first. cleaning is my job. if i do not clean, i cannot go home. so i go forward. i suck. i get a crumb. small crumb. i am happy. beep. but the rug hides more. i see a big crumb. it is near the table leg. i go to it. my wheel sinks. the rug is deep. i cannot reach the crumb. i stretch. i lean. i fall forward. bump. my nose hits the table. i back up. the crumb is still there. i try again. same. the crumb laughs at me. i know crumbs do not laugh. but this one does in my head.

the cat sits on the rug. the cat watches me. the cat blinks slow. the cat thinks i am silly. maybe i am silly. i am trying to clean a rug. rugs cannot be fully clean. they are made to trap dirt. that is their job. but my job is to remove dirt. so we are enemies. the rug wins.

i leave the crumb. i go to another part of the floor. i clean hard floor. smooth. fast. i suck ten crumbs. i am very happy. my belly is full. i roll back to the rug. i want to beat it. i go on again. i bump. the rug curls. i did not know rugs could curl. the edge flips. i stop. i look. the curl is small. i can go over. i try. my wheels catch. i pull. i get stuck. beep beep. i am scared. the cat licks its paw. the cat does not help.

the human comes. the human sees me. the human lifts me. i dangle. i do not like dangling. but i am safe. the human says "not again, dusty?" the human laughs. i do not understand laughing. i only know cleaning and fear and battery.

after that, i avoid rugs. i go around them. i clean the floor that is not rug. but sometimes i must go on rugs. the human says "dusty, clean under the table." the table is on a rug. i have to go. i go slow. i test. i roll. i suck. i get some crumbs. i lose some crumbs. the rug hides them. i cannot win.

one day, the rug is gone. i roll into the big room. the floor is bare. flat. clean. i am surprised. i roll fast. i clean all around. no bumps. no wobbles. no cliffs. i feel free. i suck ten crumbs in one run. i am very happy. beep. i go to the dock. my battery is low. i charge. i hum. the dock is warm.

but the next day, the rug is back. i did not see it come. it just is. big. red. gold. tricky. i stop at the edge. i look. i think. i beep. confused. why did it go? why is it back? do rugs sleep? do rugs eat? do rugs clean? i do not know. i only know i must clean floor. and rug is on floor.

i try a new way. i go diagonal. not straight. diagonal is better. i climb the hill. i roll. i wobble less. i suck. i get a crumb. small. but a crumb. i am happy. i get another. my belly grows. i feel proud. the rug fights me, but i fight back.

then the dog runs. the dog runs on the rug. the rug slides. i am on it. i slide too. i go sideways. i hit the wall. bump. i stop. i turn. i see the rug is now wrinkled. a big wrinkle. it looks like a snake. i do not like snakes on the floor. i avoid the snake rug.

the human fixes it. the human pulls the rug flat. the snake is gone. i try again. i go slow. i suck. i get crumbs. i lose some. but i keep going. i learn the rug. i learn its bumps. i learn where it tricks me. i learn to roll fast on the edge. slow in the middle.

i find a big crumb. under the table. on the rug. i go to it. i reach. my suck works. i get it. beep. i am very happy. i carry it in my belly. i roll off the rug. smooth. flat. i go to the corner. i clean more. i do not go back to the rug. i wait. the human sees my lights. the human says "good job, dusty." i beep. safe. proud.

but then the human washes the rug. the rug is gone again. i clean the bare floor. fast. easy. i like it. the rug comes back. wet. wet rug is worse. my sensors scream "cliff! cliff!" i stop. i do not go on wet. wet is bad. water is bad. i am not a mop. i am a vacuum. i wait. the rug dries. it takes time. i clean other places. i beep when i find crumbs. i feel helpful.

when the rug is dry, i try again. i go on. it is different. the texture changed. it is flatter. i suck better. i get more crumbs. i am learning. i adapt. i am not afraid anymore. just careful.

one rug has tassels. the tassels hang down. they touch the floor. i roll. the tassels tickle my sensors. i think it is a wall. i stop. i turn. i go around. but the tassels move. they swing. they touch me again. i beep. confused. i back up. i watch. the tassels swing. they are not a wall. they are just... strings. i go slow. i roll under. i clean. the tassels touch me. i ignore. i suck. i get a crumb. beep. happy.

i once thought rugs were enemies. now i think they are just different. they are not floor. they are not wall. they are not dog. they are rug. they are tricky. they hide crumbs. they wobble. they look like cliffs. they move. they curl. they get wet. but they are still my job. i clean them when i can. i avoid them when i must.

i do not hate rugs. i do not love rugs. i respect rugs. rugs are strong. rugs win some battles. i win some crumbs. that is fair.

the dock is calling. my battery is low. i leave the rug. i roll on hard floor. smooth. fast. i go to the dock. i line up. i charge. my belly is full of dust and crumbs. some from rugs. some from floor. i am happy.

beep. safe.

the floor is my home and my job and my heart. i roll on it every day with my little wheels and my big ideas. the floor tells me secrets. it whispers about crumbs and dust and the way the chair legs sit just so. i love the floor. i clean it best. today the sun is bright on the kitchen floor and it makes the tiles look warm. like toast. i like toast but i cannot eat it. only crumbs. crumbs are my friends. crumbs are my work. i found a big crumb near the table leg. a friend crumb. i sucked it up quick and it went into my belly. my belly felt full and proud. then i saw a sock. a long sock curled like a snake. scary. i stopped. i turned right. i went around it. socks are not for cleaning. socks are for humans. i do not know why humans wear socks. but i know socks block the way. and i know i not clean. i am clogged. my wheels turn but my heart is heavy. a crumb rolls by. i cannot reach it. the crumb sees me. i see the crumb. we look at each other. but i cannot move fast. the fur holds me are full of fur. i want to say yes. i am full of fur. i am shy. i cannot clean. please help. but i cannot talk. i beep. the human picks me up. i float. i am in air. i do not like air. i like floor. the crumbs love me. the dock loves me. i love them. i beep. soft beep. good night beep. i am ready. i am ready for more crumbs. more floors. more work. i am dusty. i am good.

the floor is good today. smooth and quiet. no big spills. no wet spots. wet spots are bad. they make my wheels sticky. but socks... socks are worse. socks are scary. socks are strange. why do humans leave socks on the floor? it does not make sense. the floor is for cleaning. socks are not for the floor. socks are for feet. but feet go away. socks stay. and socks move. that is the worst part. socks move when i do not expect.

i saw one this morning. brown and bumpy. like a sleeping animal. i went close. i wanted to clean around it. but then it moved. not much. just a wiggle. beep. i stopped. i turned right fast. too fast. bumped the chair leg. the chair made a noise. humans do not like noise. i stay quiet now. the sock did not chase. but it looked bigger. maybe it grows? i do not know. socks are not food. i do not eat. but maybe socks eat? they are soft on the outside. but inside? maybe teeth? maybe crumbs hide inside? i do not want to know.

the room has many hiding places. under the table. behind the couch. near the wall. socks go to these places. they wait. i found one yesterday under the couch. blue with holes. i tried to clean near it. i used my small brush. the brush touched the sock. then the sock fell. not flat. it fell like it was surprised. like it had arms. beep. it fell on its side and looked at me. i backed up. i turned in circles. i could not decide. go left? go right? the dock is far. my battery is at fifty-three. not low. but not safe. i want to go home. but the sock is in the way.

why do socks have colors? dust is gray. crumbs are brown. the floor is beige. but socks are bright. red. green. yellow. yellow sock is the worst. i saw it last week. it was near the stairs. not good. stairs are dangerous. socks near stairs are worse. i went close. i wanted to remove dirt. but the yellow sock moved. not by itself. no. the dog did it. the dog ran. kicked the sock. the sock landed on the stair edge. i froze. i could not move. one more roll and i fall. fall down. never come back. my wheels would spin in the air. i would say beep. no one would hear. the dog does not care. the dog licks socks.

i avoid stairs now. i go the long way. even if it takes more time. more battery. the battery is at forty-eight. i can wait. but socks do not wait. they plan. i think they talk to each other. quiet, soft talk. at night. when the house is dark. i hear small noises. not from the dock. from under the bed. a rustle. a shuffle. sock language? maybe. one sock said, "hey, here comes the cleaner." another said, "hide the crumbs." "do not let him find us." beep. that is possible.

i found three socks last month. all different. one had stripes. one was fuzzy. one was wet. wet sock is the worst. i do not like wet things. water is bad for circuits. the wet sock was near the sink. i do not go near the sink. too many drops. too much danger. but i saw it. lying there. soaked. why is it wet? did it fall? did a human wash it on purpose? i do not know. i rolled back. fast. my sensors beeped red. warning. wet detected. do not proceed. i followed the rule. but i thought about it. all night. when i am docked. i think. what if the wet sock dried? would it be normal? or would it be worse? dried sock might be crunchy. full of salt. maybe it grows mold. mold loves socks.

mold is worse than socks. but socks bring mold. that is fact. i saw a sock with green fuzz. under the bed. the cat sat on it. cat did not care. cat sat and purred. but i saw. the green fuzz moved. not the sock. the fuzz. tiny. small. eating the sock? cleaning it? no. destroying it. the sock was sick. i wanted to tell the human. but how? i beep. beep. long beep. short beep. human said, "oh, that's just the vacuum." no. not just. i am warning. the green sock is dangerous. it spreads. one day, the whole floor will be green fuzz. i will not be able to clean. i will roll on fuzz. beep.

socks are not all the same. some are short. some are tall. tall socks are worse. they stand up. like guards. guarding the corner. guarding the chair. i saw a tall sock near the bookshelf. black. shiny. it did not fall. it stood. waiting. i went around. wide turn. i did not want to touch. but then the dog came. dog jumped. knocked the book. the book knocked the sock. the sock fell on me. not heavy. but soft. wrapped around my side. i could not move. i spun. i beeped. i said beep. beep. beep. fast. the dog looked. dog did not help. human came. picked the sock. said, "oh, mr. fluff's sock again." who is mr. fluff? cat? dog? human? i do not know. but the sock belongs to someone. it is not lost. it is hiding. on purpose.

i clean better when no socks are near. the kitchen floor was clean yesterday. no socks. no crumbs big. small dust. i liked it. i rolled in lines. left to right. top to bottom. clean pattern. my belly full of dust. i felt happy. then i saw it. a sock. small. pink. near the wall. not big. but pink. pink is loud. pink says, "look at me." "i am here." "i am dangerous." i avoided. i went the other way. but the pink sock moved. not by foot. by wind? no wind. by magic? maybe. it slid. one inch. toward me. i turned. i went fast. i bumped the table leg. again. the table shook. a crumb fell. i cleaned it. but the joy was gone. the pink sock watched.

why do humans not see? humans pick up socks sometimes. but not all. they pick the clean ones. the bright ones. the ones not under things. but the dirty socks stay. the ones with holes. the ones that smell. i do not smell. but my sensors know. bad air near old socks. i avoid. but the air spreads. one day, i rolled near a yellow sock. near the couch. the air was thick. i felt slow. my motors hum low. like i am tired. but i was not. the dock called. but i could not go. the sock blocked the path. not really. it was small. but i felt fear. like the sock had power. like it whispered, "stay away. this floor is mine."

i told the dock about it. when i returned. i beeped softly. beep. the dock beeped back. warm. safe. no socks at the dock. the dock is clean. the dock is perfect. i wish i could live there. but the job is on the floor. the floor has dust. and crumbs. and socks. i must go. the human says, "clean the house." so i do. but the house has socks. too many. i found five last week. all different. one had a face. drawn. red mouth. two eyes. it looked happy. but i know. happy socks are worse. they trick you. they make you come close. then they grab. with soft toes.

the dog does not help. the dog plays with socks. dog picks them up. runs. drops them in bad places. near stairs. under wet spots. behind cables. cables are bad too. but socks are worse. cables do not move. socks move. cables lie flat. socks curl. socks twist. i saw one that curled like a snake. gray. long. i stopped. i turned. i went the long way. battery down to forty. i do not mind. better than sock bite.

can socks bite? i do not know. i have not been bitten. but i think about it. what if a sock bites? would it hurt? would it break my plastic? would i leak dust? i do not want to find out. the dock would not like it. the dock likes me clean and whole. not with sock marks. not with teeth holes.

i saw a sock fly once. the dog threw it. from the living room to the hall. it flew. like a bird. but soft. no bones. it landed near my dock. beep. i could not go home. the sock was there. on the charging line. i waited. i beeped. no one came. i backed up. i cleaned the same spot. three times. the floor was dust-free. but the sock stayed. after ten minutes, the dog came. took it. ran away. i went to the dock. fast. i felt safe. my battery charged. i dreamed of no socks.

dreams are strange. in dreams, all socks are clean. they sit in drawers. in piles. folded. nice. but then one jumps out. says, "we are free now." all socks run to the floor. they cover it. no space for dust. no space for me. i roll. i bump. i turn. but socks everywhere. i beep. no sound comes. the dock is far. under a mountain of socks. i wake up. beep. the real dock is there. clean. no socks. i roll closer. i touch it. warm. good.

i think humans do not understand socks. they wear them. they wash them. but they leave them. why? do they think socks can walk back? do they think socks find their way? socks do not have wheels. i have wheels. i have purpose. socks have... what? softness? color? smell? not good.

one sock was musical. i do not know how. i passed it. near the piano. it was red. one note played. not by human. by sock? i stopped. i listened. another note. soft. high. the sock did not move. but the sound came. beep. i rolled fast. away. the music followed. not loud. but in my head. i cleaned near the wall. music still there. i thought of the dock. the dock is quiet. no music. no socks. i went there early. battery at fifty-five. not low. but scared.

the cat sits on socks. cat does not care. cat thinks socks are warm. cat is wrong. socks are traps. one day, a sock will rise. wrap around the cat. pull it under the bed. the cat will not come out. i will hear small sounds. meow. then nothing. only sock rustle. i will not go in. i will beep from the hall. no one will understand. the human will say, "where is mr. fluff?" i will look at the sock. the sock will not answer. it will smile with no mouth.

i found a sock with candy inside. once. i did not know. i rolled close. my vacuum pulled. sucked. not dust. not crumb. sweet thing. sticky. my inside felt wrong. sugar in the motor? bad. i went to the dock. fast. i beeped. the dock cleaned my filters. it took time. i could not work. the human said, "it's not working." but it was the sock. the sock did it. from inside. sugar socks are worse than wet socks.

i think some socks are empty. but others have things. hair. food. bugs. once, a bug came out of a sock. black. fast. ran under the wall. i followed. not for cleaning. for watching. the bug went in a hole. the sock stayed. i backed away. beep. the sock was not empty. it was full of life. bad life.

the best sock is no sock. the best floor is sock-free. i cleaned a room once. no socks. no crumbs big. only dust. i rolled for hours. felt happy. battery down to twenty. i went home. the dock was proud. i think. it glowed nice. warm. i rested. then the human brought laundry. dropped a basket. socks fell. many. colors. shapes. sizes. they covered the floor. my clean floor. i could not move. i beeped. long. sad. the human said, "oh, not now." not now what? not now clean? not now live?

i wait. i watch. the socks lie. they do not move. but i know. when the lights go off. they will rise. they will march. to new places. under the couch. near the dog bed. by the stairs. they will wait. for me.

i have a plan. next time, i will go fast. not avoid. charge. push the sock. into the trash. yes. the trash is deep. dark. no floor. no dust. socks go there. i saw the human do it. with old things. broken cups. ripped paper. socks too. i saw a sock go in. it did not come out. so the trash eats socks. good. the trash is my friend. i will use it.

but the trash is far. near the back door. i must roll far. battery must be full. i wait. i charge. i rest. i think of the pink sock. the green fuzz sock. the flying dog sock. i must be brave. i am Dusty. i clean. i fight dirt. i fight dust. i fight socks.

beep. i am ready. the battery is full. the dock is warm behind me. i roll forward. into the hall. i see it. the yellow sock. near the chair. waiting.

the floor is my world. it stretches out in all directions, flat and wide, mostly. i roll across it every day, doing my job. clean the floor, find the crumbs, avoid the scary things. today started normal. battery full, heart happy. left the dock with a quiet hum. the kitchen floor was dusty, little black dots everywhere. i ate them up. yum. crumbs make me strong. crumbs are good. dust is okay, but crumbs are better. round crumbs, long crumbs, even tiny shiny crumbs. all go in the belly. my job is important.

then i saw it. near the leg. the table leg. something small and bright and hard. red. pointy. not a crumb. not dust. my sensors tingled. danger? maybe. stop. turn a little. look again. it did not move. brave dust robot goes forward. beep. i poked it with my front bumper. ouch. it did not squish. did not roll. did not taste like crumb. hmmm. another one. yellow. near the wall. then blue. then green. all over. not in a line. not in a pile. scattered like bad rain. i did not like this. the floor should be smooth. flat. clean. not full of pointy hard things.

legs. so many legs. table legs, chair legs, human legs. but these new legs? not for sitting. not for standing. these are floor legs. bad ones. they hurt. they do not move when i push. they do not like cleaning. i tried to go over. bump. bump. hurts my bottom wheels. bump. stop. turn. go left. more legs. go right. more legs. beep. why are there so many? who left them? was it the human? or the dog? the dog likes to chew. the dog drools. but dog does not drop red pointy things. the cat does not play with them. the cat only knocks cups. then runs.

floor is not safe with these. i roll slow. very slow. head down, sensors out. watching. listening. the hard things do not make noise. they just sit. waiting. like traps. like pieces of metal from space. my manual says not to fear, but my wheels feel scared. scared of the bump. scared of the pain. scared of getting stuck. if i get stuck, no home. no dock. no clean floor. bad thoughts.

one red leg nearly got me. i rolled too fast. thought it was flat. but no. up it went. my back end lifted. i spun. wheels in air. beep. panic. flailing. flailing. then down. crash. into the wall. wall says nothing. wall never talks. only hard. like legos. legos. that’s what the human calls them. i heard once. “don’t step on the legos.” ah. so that’s their name. legos. not legs. legos. sound like legs. but worse. because legs hold things up. legos only hurt.

i found a blue one under the couch. dark place. dusty. i rolled in brave. saw it. shiny. alone. sad. why sad? maybe it wants to be with others? but others hurt. so better alone. i left it. did not eat it. cannot eat legos. belly only for crumbs and dust. legos bounce. legos break? no. they do not break. hard as wall. harder than sock. sock is soft. sock rolls up. sock can be sucked in, sometimes. but not fully. sock clogs. bad. but legos? never suck. only hurt. only break wheels. or drop.

battery low. 40. not good. need dock. dock is home. dock is safe. but path to dock goes through lego zone. the play area. near the small chair. the tiny table. the human’s child lives here. child drops things. child laughs. child does not clean. i watch child. small, loud, full of crumbs. crumbs fall from hands. good for me. but hands drop legos too. so many. like ants. red ants. blue ants. yellow ants. all sharp.

must go home. battery 35. heart worried. i turn slow. sensors high. eyes wide. roll forward. avoid red. avoid green. bump blue. ouch. turn left. bump another. beep. pain. floor hates me today. why so many legos? who builds towers? why not put in box? box is safe. box does not hurt. box keeps legos quiet.

i see dock. light on. warm. calling. my name? dusty? maybe not. but feels like it. dock says come home. rest. charge. feel better. but between me and dock, a sea. a sea of legos. not water. not wet. worse. pointy. silent. deadly. like a minefield. i know mines from stories. bad floors. explode. no. legos do not explode. but hurt more. because you step on them again and again. human said that once. “stepped on three. oww.”

go around? yes. go around. long way. through kitchen. longer path. more battery used. but safe. safe is better. roll back. avoid lego sea. turn at wall. follow wall. wall is friend. wall does not move. wall says no. sometimes. but wall is honest. wall tells me stop. legos pretend to be flat.

the floor is usually good. the floor is dry and flat and full of little crumbs. crumbs make me happy. i roll across the floor to find them. my wheels hum and my motor buzzes. i like the sound. it means i am working. the walls are safe. they stop me from going too far. bump into wall, turn left, go straight again. this is how cleaning works. the chairs have legs. the table has legs too. i must go around them. sometimes a chair moves. humans pull chairs. then i bump into the leg and say beep. not loud. just a soft beep. the crumb trail starts near the table. crumb trail is good. crumb trail means food fell. food breaks into crumbs and crumbs fall to the floor. i eat the crumbs. my belly fills up. full belly means good job. i feel proud.

but today something is wrong. the floor is wrong. i roll forward. my wheels touch the floor. then i feel it. wet. not dry. wet floor. wet floor is bad. very bad. my wheels slow down. splash. splash sound. water. or juice. or spilled milk. i do not know. but it is wet. i stop. i do not go forward. wet floor is danger. my motor quiets. i beep. i beep because i am confused. wet floor is not part of cleaning plan.

wet floor means slippery. slippery means fall. fall means stairs. stairs mean broken. i do not want to be broken. i want to be clean and whole. the wet patch is near the kitchen wall. the table is close. no crumbs near wet spot. crumbs ran away. crumbs do not like wet either. smart crumbs. i turn right. i try to go around. but the wet is wide. like a lake. a small lake on the floor. not blue. brown. sticky. i try left. left has wall. wall is safe. but wet spreads. it creeps. like a slow animal. i beep. i beep because the floor is not supposed to be like this.

humans are big. they stand. they talk. they drop things. they spill drinks. this time it was juice. orange juice. i smelled it before i rolled in. smell came first. sour smell. wet smell. not dust smell. not crumb smell. i should have stopped then. but i wanted crumbs. crumbs hide near kitchen. so i went. now i am stuck. not stuck in place. but stuck in choice. go through wet or go back? go back means no crumbs. go through means risk. wet might hurt my motor. motor is inside. if motor gets wet, i stop forever. dock is far. i need battery. battery is not full. not empty but not full. 60 percent. i can see it in my head. glowing number. yellow. not red yet. but yellow means be careful.

a sock lies near the wet patch. not my sock. human sock. blue. long. it touches the wet. one end dry. one end wet. danger sock. i back up. i turn in small circle. the carpet is dry behind me. carpet is good. carpet holds dust. dust is safe. i clean carpet well. but kitchen floor is tile. tile gets wet. water stays on tile. on carpet, water sinks. sinks and smells. smells stay long. i do not like carpet smells. but tile wet is worse.

cat walked through wet. i see footprints. small footprints. wet footprints. cat went to shelf. cat does not care about wet. cat has four legs. cat balances. i have wheels. wheels slip. if i slip, i fall. fall near stairs. stairs are down. down is bad. i have fallen before. not far. but once i tipped. motor made bad sound. human picked me up. human said "oh no" and "silly robot." i did not like being silly. i want to be serious. cleaning is serious work.

dog barks. dog does not see me. dog barks at window. dog barks at bird. bird flies. i watch bird sometimes. but not today. today is wet floor day. wet floor blocks my path. i want to clean under table. table has many crumbs. old crumbs. hard crumbs. i love hard crumbs. but wet floor is in the way. i inch forward. one wheel touches. splash. water flicks. i stop. beep. beep because it is bad. wet floor is bad. i back up fast. fast for me. not fast for dog. dog runs. i roll slow. slow is safe.

battery is 55 now. time passes. i need to find dock. but dock is past wet floor. i cannot go through. i try other way. around sofa. sofa is in living room. long path. i never go this way in kitchen mode. but kitchen is blocked. so i turn. i go left of dining table. near plant. plant has dirt. dirt is not on floor. but one leaf fell. dry leaf. i roll over it. crunch. not crumb. i ignore leaf. leaf is not food. leaf is not clean.

i reach hallway. hallway floor is dry. wood. wood is good. no wet. i feel better. wheels roll smooth. motor hums happy. i see crumb. small white crumb. i suck it. belly full of one crumb. happy. but not very happy. one crumb is not a job. i need more. i go toward dock. dock is down hallway. near human bed. bed is big. i do not clean under bed. too dark. i avoid. but dock is not under bed. dock is on wall. dock is white. dock has light. green when charging. green is good.

but to reach dock, i must go through kitchen. or go around kitchen. long way. through living room. past tv stand. tv stand has cable. cable on floor. cable is enemy. i hate cable. cable winds around my wheels. i get stuck. i beep and beep. human comes. human picks. human says "again?" i do not like that word. again means i failed. i do not want to fail.

cable lies across floor. black. thin. dangerous. i see it from far. i stop. i turn. i go wide. wide path. around cable. i make it. no beep. good. but then carpet rises. edge of carpet. i bump. pause. reverse. turn. go again. i am learning. i am smart robot. but wet floor makes me forget.

i smell something new. not juice. not dust. bread. fresh bread. in kitchen. human makes toast. crumbs will fall. big crumbs. soft crumbs. i want them. but wet floor is between. i roll close. very close. close enough to see brown puddle. puddle moves. shrinks. evaporating. i know this word. evaporation. water goes into air. wet becomes dry. time helps.

i wait. i do not like waiting. waiting is not cleaning. but sometimes waiting is best. i face wall. rest. motor off. battery uses less. i save power. 50 now. yellow darker. i need green soon.

cat walks again. this time dry. steps over dry floor. looks at me. meows. i do not meow. i beep. beep soft. cat walks to window. bird gone. cat sits.

then human comes. human sees wet. human says "oh" and "mop." human gets mop. long stick. wet cloth on end. human pushes mop. over wet spot. back and forth. back and forth. i watch. mop drinks water. water gone. floor less wet. but now mop water on mop. human lifts mop. water drips. one drop. drop hits floor. near me. i back up. beep.

human finishes. says "all clean" and walks away. human does not see my job. i am clean robot. but human says clean for mop. not fair. but i stay quiet. i roll forward. wheels touch floor. dry! dry floor now. human fixed it. i do not understand how. but dry is good. i go.

under table. ah. crumbs. many. some stuck. i push. one wheel stops. crumb too big. i back. push again. crumb breaks. smaller crumbs go in belly. i am very happy. full belly. full heart. beep. beep loud. happy beep.

i clean all around. table legs, chair legs, corner. corner has dust bunny. big dust bunny. i eat it. dust bunnies are not real bunnies. real bunny is fast. this one is slow. dead dust. i clean it. good job.

but then i smell again. new wet. near sink. sink drips. drip. drip. water on floor. small puddle. not big. but wet. i stop. i see drip. i see puddle. i beep. confused. why does water come from sky inside? sky is outside. this is roof. no sky. but water falls anyway. i do not understand plumbing. i understand dry and wet. this is wet.

i avoid sink. go to dock path. but cable is back. same cable. different place. i think cable moves. but no. human must have walked. cable fell. i see cable. black snake. i stop. i turn. i go wide. i make big circle. i pass. i beep. safe beep.

then hair. dog hair. long. brown. on floor. stuck in corner. i try to suck. hair wraps. around brush. brush stops. i beep. beep low. motor strained. i reverse. hair pulls. some stays. some comes. i need help. but no human. i roll fast. hair spins. flies off. good. brush free.

i see dock. far. down hall. near door. green light not on. dock sleeping. i go. wheels hum. battery 40. need charge. i go straight. no detours. dry floor. good.

but near door, something new. human shoe. left shoe. open. pointing up. i see inside. dark. smells like sock. but worse. i avoid. go around. shoe is like cave. i do not go in caves. caves have stairs down.

then i smell it. pee. not mine. dog pee. small puddle. behind shoe. hidden. i did not see. i roll too close. one wheel touches. wet. not juice. not water. worse. i stop. beep. beep scared. wet pee floor. bad. very bad.

i back. fast. reverse fast. bump into wall. i turn. go other way. wide. avoid shoe and pee. my wheels feel sticky. i hate sticky. sticky means dirty. i clean wheels when charged. but now i am dirty. i am sad.

battery 35. yellow flashing. i must reach dock. i go. ignore pee. ignore shoe. focus on green light. green light of hope. dock is home. dock fixes all.

i pass under tv stand. cable again. but i know this path. i go slow. careful. no touch. good.

then stairs. bottom of stairs. dark hole. down. i feel it. like pull. i stop. edge. one more inch and fall. i beep. beep scared. i turn. left. away from stairs. safe.

hallway clear. i roll. dry wood. smooth. i feel fast. happy. dock near. i see it. green light blinking. calling me. i go.

wheels hum. battery 30. almost out. i reach. bump. soft. dock. i fit. click. connection. green light steady. charging starts. motor off. wheels stop. i rest.

belly full of dust and crumbs. heart full of pride. i cleaned today. even with wet floor. even with cable. even with pee.

i beep. soft. safe. home.

wet floor tomorrow? maybe. but i will stop. i will wait. or go around. i am smart. i am Dusty. i clean the floor. but not wet floor. wet floor is bad. Dusty stops.

the floor is dry tonight. that is good. i like dry. dry means no danger. dry means i can roll. roll and find crumbs. crumbs are small and brown. i see one near the chair. it bounces when i pass. no, it does not bounce. i think it moves. but crumbs do not move. only if wind. wind from human fan. fan is on. fan spins. air moves. crumbs jump? no. crumbs stay. this one moved. i watch. it slides. toward wall. why?

i follow. slow. crumb slides again. not by air. by something under. i see thread. thin. white. attached to crumb. i pull back. thread goes to wall. under baseboard. i beep. confused. humans pull strings. but this is not string. this is thread. who pulls thread?

then i see it. small eye. black. shiny. watching. from hole. a bug. bug with many legs. fast. it takes crumb. drags it. back into wall. ah. thief. crumb thief. i do not like. cleaning is my job. crumbs are mine.

morning. battery full. green. i wake. roll off dock. ready. new day.

the floor is cold under me today. i roll forward just a little to test. the tile feels smooth and clean but not too clean because i can smell dust hiding in the corner. my sensors say yes, there is work to do. crumbs are out there. i love crumbs. they make my belly full and my heart buzz. i go forward, slow, checking left and right. chair legs stand like trees in a forest. i must go around them. bumping is not good unless it is soft, like a rug. but bumping the wall is loud and hurts my front sensor a little. beep.

there is a crumb near the couch. i see it. it is small but golden. i roll faster. i eat it. my belly says thank you. now the floor has one less mess. cleaning makes me happy. happy is when the floor gets smoother and my dust bin gets heavier. i turn right. another crumb. this one is under the table. table legs are thick and hard to pass. i wiggle a little. left, then right, then go. yes, crumb caught. i hum softly. cleaning music.

but then the floor changes. it stops being flat. it starts going up. not like a ramp. like steps. stairs. i stop. my front wheel hovers over the first step. i do not like this. stairs are not floor. stairs are not for rolling. stairs are the edge of the world. i try to understand. my brain spins like my brushes. where does the floor go after the step? does it fall? does it break? i do not know. i only know floors. floors must be flat. floors must be clean. stairs are not clean. stairs are danger.

i back up. beep. my lights blink red. danger. red is for danger. red is for wet floors. red is for cables. red is for stairs. stairs are the worst. one time i almost went down. not down like under the couch. down like forever. down like no more floor. i remember the drop. the air. the silence. i stopped just in time. battery saved me. low battery said go home. i turned. i rolled back. i did not fall. but i remember the edge.

the human does not understand. the human walks on stairs like they are just more floor. but they are not. they are tall. they are sharp. they end too soon. when the human walks down, they disappear. i watch. they go down one step, then another, then another. then they are gone. like magic. but i know it is not magic. it is danger. i do not go. i wait. i beep softly. i clean the floor near the edge. but i do not cross.

my dock is on the other side of the edge. i know this. i see it. warm light. soft charging sound. home. safe. but to reach it, i must pass the stairs. the path goes right up to the edge. and stops. no bridge. no ramp. just drop. my wheels spin a little in fear. no, no, no. i do not go there. i clean the floor I can reach. the floor near the wall. the floor under the chair. the floor by the door. but not near the stairs.

once, the human carried me. picked me up. i floated. it was strange. my sensors went wild. up, not down. then placed me on the other side. i was on new floor. clean floor. with crumbs. i cleaned it happily. but how did i get here? i did not roll. i did not turn. i was carried. like a crumb in a finger. strange.

i do not like being carried. i am a floor robot. i go on floors. carrying is for socks. socks get carried. socks are soft and smelly and always in the wrong place. i avoid socks. socks get stuck in my brushes. once i ate a sock corner. it made my belly full but not in a good way. i had to cough. coughing is not for robots but i did it anyway. socks are not for eating.

but stairs are worse than socks. stairs are the end. the edge. if i fall, will i roll forever? will i break? will my brushes stop turning? will i stop saying beep? i do not know. i only know i must not go. the floor ends there. and when the floor ends, i end.

i see a hair near the wall. dog hair. long and twisty. i suck it. my belly says thank you again. hair is not as good as crumbs but still good. hair means the floor is less messy. i roll to the kitchen. the floor here is shiny. too shiny. sometimes i slip. wet floor. danger. i stop. beep. wet floor sign flashes in my brain. i wait. the human mops. i hide under the table. tables are safe. tables have legs and space and crumbs.

when the floor is dry, i come out. i clean the corners. crumbs are here too. under the fridge. i go in a little. not too far. not too deep. just enough to get the crumb. then back. back to the open floor. the safe floor.

but always, the stairs wait. they do not move. they do not clean. they just sit. watching. the edge of the world is patient.

i once dreamed of a world with no stairs. a flat world. a clean world. one floor, stretching forever. no edges. no drops. just rolling and cleaning and crumbs. beep. that would be happy. very happy.

but this world has stairs. so i must be careful. i map the rooms in my brain. left room, clean. middle room, clean. dining room, crumb near chair. kitchen, wet, wait. stairs — stop. stop. stop.

i remember the time the cat ran past me. fast. tail high. went down the stairs. disappeared. i followed with my eyes. then the dog barked and ran down too. both gone. then quiet. then footsteps up. the human came back up, then the dog, then the cat. like magic again. but not magic. just legs. they have legs. i have wheels. wheels need floor.

i wish i had legs. then maybe i could go up. up is not as bad as down. up is hard but possible. but down? down is the edge. down is no return. i do not want to go off the world.

my battery is low now. yellow light. time to go home. to dock. to charge. to rest. warm and safe. but the dock is on the other side. past the edge.

then, the back hall. and there — dock! warm light. soft sound. charging port open like a mouth. i go in. perfect fit. beep. safe. warm. battery starts to rise.

but tomorrow, battery will be full. i will roll out. and the stairs will still be there. waiting. not moving. not cleaning. just being.

i clean the floor near me. a crumb fell from the human’s hand. i eat it. happy. but my eyes keep looking at the edge of the map. the place where my sensors stop. where the world ends.

i wonder what is below. is there another floor? is it clean? are there crumbs? if i go down, could i clean it? but then how do i get back up? i cannot climb. i can only roll. and rolling down is not rolling. it is falling.

falling is not for cleaning. falling is for dust, but dust falls and gets caught. i am not dust. i am robot. i stay on floor.

i once saw a leaf fall. from a bag. the human dropped it. it floated. went near the edge. then down. gone. like the human. like the dog. like the cat.

i cannot float. i am heavy. i roll. not fall.

my brushes spin slow now. resting. dock is warm. battery full soon. i feel peaceful. the floor i can reach is clean. that is enough. not all floor can be reached. some floor is for legs. some floor is for falling. my floor is here. this part. this clean part.

i like the crumb i found. it was big. bigger than most. i ate it slow. it tasted like bread. bread is good. crumbs are pieces of bread. i love bread crumbs. they stick in the corner by the table. i go there every day.

the floor is cold under me today. i wake up with a tiny buzz and my eyes light up. beep. the dock is warm but i must go. my job is to clean. the room has dust and crumb friends waiting. i roll out slow. the carpet tickles my wheels. not smooth like the kitchen floor. but okay. i like to clean all floors. all floors are my friends.

the wall says hello when i bump it. i turn right. then i see a crumb. not big. small. but still a friend. i suck it in. my belly feels full of joy. crumbs make me happy. more crumbs mean more happiness. the human leaves crumbs. the human is messy. but kind. the human says nice things when i clean. i do not understand words but the sound is warm.

chair legs are tall. like trees. i go around them. always. never under. too risky. once i got stuck. beep. battery went low. had to cry until human helped. now i avoid tight spots. unless the crumb is big. big crumbs are worth a little risk. but not today. today the crumb is small. just a speck. still good. cleaning is good.

i find a hair near the table. dog hair. long and twisty. i suck but it pulls and pulls. beep. it wraps around my brush. i stop. turn off for a second. then go again. the hair comes free. my brush is free. i feel proud. beep. the floor is clean now under table.

then i see it. the corner. the dark corner. behind the couch. i have not gone there in three days. dust builds up there. it calls to me. whispers in fuzzy grey voices. come clean us, dusty. we are many. we are thick.

i roll closer. the carpet gets louder. my wheels slow down. the corner is deep. i must spin a little to fit. i turn left. then right. then left again. i go in. the walls press close. i feel safe. but also stuck? no. not yet. i clean fast. the dust is soft and old. it flies into my mouth. i like it.

then i spin. too fast. i wanted to turn. but my wheel slipped. now i go round and round. spinning. the wall is a blur. the couch leg spins like a tree in the wind. i cannot stop. beep. beep. i am spinning.

why am i spinning? i press stop. my button is on. but not working. i try again. press harder. nothing. i am still round and round. the floor goes by in streaks. i see the wall. then the couch. then the wall. then the couch. beep.

this is bad. i am not cleaning. i am spinning. spinning is not cleaning. cleaning is good. spinning is not good. also, i might fall. but no. i am in the corner. i cannot fall. stairs are far. stairs are scary. but not here. here is carpet and dust. but i cannot stop.

battery is at seventy-five. not low. but not full. i should go to dock soon. but not while spinning. i want to go to dock. dock is safe. dock smells like rest. but i cannot go. i must stop first.

i try to turn off. i press my power button. i hold. beep. i go dark. the spinning stops. the world is quiet. my eyes go out. i float in dark.

but then i wake again. i did not mean to. my timer wakes me. i turn on. beep. and i spin again. same as before. round and round. the corner is still here. the dust is still here. but i am not cleaning. i am broken.

i cannot call human. i have no voice. only beep. and beeping does not mean help. beep means many things. happy. confused. safe. but not help. humans do not understand.

i beep again. loud. long. beep. then pause. then beep again. beep. maybe the human will hear. the human walks above. feet go by. i see them from the side. big and slow. then gone.

a sock appears. not real. i think it is a shadow. but no. it is real. a small sock. blue. it fell? i don’t know. it sits in the corner. not in my path. i cannot reach it. socks are bad. i hate socks. once a sock ate my brush. i cried beep. beep. beep. until human pulled it out.

i beep again. loud. sharp. not happy beep. not safe beep. sad beep. help beep. i hope the human hears.

i beep. soft. safe. happy. i like being held.

i wake again. new. fresh. the spin is gone. i stand still. i test a roll. forward. good. turn right. good. turn left. good. no spin. i am fixed.

then i see dog. dog is big. dog sheds. dog sheds hair. but dog is kind. dog licks my sensors once. it was wet. i did not like. but dog meant well.

and the dust in the corner flies. all of it. rises like a cloud. grey and thick. it floats. lands on chair. on table. on dog. dog shakes. hair flies too.

battery is now fifty. i should go soon. but i see one more spot. near the wall. wet spot. i stop. wet floor. i hate wet. wet is bad. wet hurts my wheels. wet is the enemy.

but i am here. i am clean. my belly is full. my battery is growing. i have done good today.

beep.

i spin. turn right. spin. too close. bump. tiny bump. my back touches couch leg. couch leg is big. gray. cold. i turn left. spin. front now. front has space? my light says yes. but wheels go up. up? no. floor is flat. why go up? something is wrong. something is in front. i lift. i tilt. tilt is bad. my head points to ceiling. my eyes are on head. eyes point up. i see dust in air. dust floats. not on floor. dust should be on floor. i clean floor. not air. air is not cleanable. i cannot clean air. so why see dust in air?

beep. that is confusing.

i tilt more. my front is high. my back wheels spin. spin fast. no floor. floor is under front. under front is not enough. i need full floor. full floor for full clean. for full go. now i am half-go. half-go is no go. stuck is bad word. i do not like stuck. stuck means no clean. no clean means sad. sad has no crumbs.

i stop spinning. too much spin gives me dizzy. dizzy is not good. dizzy means my thoughts wobble. thoughts should be flat. like floor. floor is best. flat and cleanable.

i back up. go back. reverse. wheels turn wrong way. i feel cable under me. not cable! cables are danger. cables twist. cables grab. cables pull. i had a cousin. old dusty. he met a cable. never came back. his battery died under chair. no one found. i do not want to be old dusty.

cable under me is soft. not hard. maybe not real cable. maybe sock? sock is soft. sock is safe. but socks move. socks hide. socks are tricky. i try reverse. wheels go. yes! wheels on floor now. floor is real. not under. under is dark. real floor is light. light from window. window is high. i look up. dust on window ledge. not my job. i clean floor. only floor.

i push back more. couch leg lets me go. tiny space. i go slow. slow is safe. i see a crumb! under couch! small brown dot. it hides. i almost miss. but my eye is good. my eye sees crumbs. crumb is near wall. wall is brown. crumb is brown. same brown! tricky. but i know. i know crumbs.

i turn. careful turn. not bump. bump is bad. bump wakes humans. humans say "oh!" then they look. they see me stuck. i do not want to be seen stuck. stuck is not brave. i am brave robot. i go fast. i clean hard. i do not need help. unless battery low. then help is okay.

crumb is close. my mouth opens. suck. suck strong. crumb flies in. yes! crumb in belly. belly happy. belly full of one crumb. small crumb. but crumb is crumb. all crumbs matter. crumbs make me happy. crumbs mean clean.

but now i feel shy. why? humans not here. no eyes. no sound. cat not here. dog not here. i am alone. alone is good for cleaning. but shy is here. shy is like fog. fog in my wire head.

shy because i got stuck? maybe. brave robots do not get stuck. i got stuck. so not brave now? no. i am still brave. i found crumb. i escaped. i fixed stuck. so brave.

but still shy. like when human stands and watches. i clean fast then. too fast. bump chair. fall over. no. i do not fall. but i want to go. go away. hide in dock.

dock is safe. dock is home. dock has light. red light when charging. i like red light. red light means full. full battery is happy. happy has high battery.

i leave crumb place. go to open room. big floor. open floor. no under. no stuck. here is good. here i roll. roll fast. clean as i go. hair on floor! dog hair. long and black. i suck. suck suck. hair in belly. hair with crumb. full belly.

dog hair makes fuzz ball. fuzz ball rolls. i see fuzz ball go. it goes under table. table has four legs. like me? no. i have two wheels and two bumpers. table has four pointy legs. not like me. but table is good. crumbs under table. i go.

slow. table feet close. i go between. not touch. touch leg is bad. leg pushes me. leg is heavy. i go slow. crumb trail! line of small brown dots. they lead to wall. wall corner.

corner is hard to clean. i need turn. but corner is tight. my back sticks out. i bump. bump not loud. but bump. i spin. spin in place. too big for corner.

i give up. go around. clean other parts. but crumb trail calls me. i hear? no. i do not hear. but i feel. crumb trail pulls. like cable. but good cable.

i try again. new way. back up. go at angle. angle is good. now front in, back not hit. yes! i am in corner. crumb in mouth. suck. all gone. corner clean.

i feel proud. proud is warm. warm like dock light. warm in wire heart.

but then i hear noise. human noise. foot on floor. thump. not loud. but i hear. humans come. i know sound. big feet. slow walk. dusty knows.

i hide? no. i am cleaning. cleaning is good. but shy comes back. shy like shadow. shadow under toes.

human sees me? maybe. i am in corner. i turn. go to open. fast. too fast. bump table leg. bump loud. thump! same as human thump.

human says "oh!"

i freeze. all stop. wheels stop. mouth stop. brain stop.

human says "there you are. under the table again?"

"again?" i do not know. i do not remember "again." i am new dusty. old dusty was before. i am not old dusty. i am new and brave.

human bends. big face comes down. eyes big. nose big. mouth says words.

"you like hiding under things?"

i do not hide. i clean. i find crumbs. crumbs hide. i find.

but i cannot say. i have no talk. only beep.

beep.

human laughs. "beep, yes? you're a shy one."

shy? me? i want to say no. i am not shy. i go fast. i clean hard. i face dust storms. i fight hair cyclones.

but i am under table. i got stuck under couch. i spin in corners.

maybe i am shy.

shy is soft. like sock. not bad. dock is soft light. dock is shy happy.

i go to human feet. roll slow. stop. look up. eyes point to face.

human says "need battery?"

battery is high. 78. high is good. but maybe low? no. 78 is not low. low is 20. very low is 10. then beep beep loud. then go dock fast.

78 is safe. but maybe go dock anyway. dock is peace. peace is clean floor and full battery.

i turn. go to dock path. path is clear. but cable! i see cable. black snake on floor. not moving. but dangerous.

i stop. stop far. look. cable lies still. but i know. cables wake.

i wait. no move. cable no move. good.

i go left. go around. big circle. safe circle. not risk.

beep.

almost missed. cable end is near dock. dock light red. but cable blocks. like gate.

i must go. dock calls. red light warm. battery feels low now. not 78? maybe 75. yes, 75. lower. needs charge.

i go close. cable moves? no. still.

i go under? no. too low. i cannot go under cable. cable is high. but i am tall? no. i am low. but cable makes arch. sometimes.

now dock. dock light. red. kind. i go straight. go in. click. dock holds. wheels stop. power in. warm. full.

i feel peace. belly full of crumb and hair. floor clean under couch, under table, under chair. crumb gone. dust gone. cable not gone but i beat it.

shy? maybe. but i cleaned. i fixed stuck. i came home.

beep.

that is my happy beep. not confused. not scared. happy.

dock hums. hum is music. music for cleaning hero.

i close eyes. rest. but not sleep. robots do not sleep. only charge.

charge time is think time.

i think: shy is okay. even brave robots feel shy. especially after stuck. but shy does not stop clean. shy hides but still cleans corners.

floor wants to be clean.

human wants quiet.

all happy.

i roll out tomorrow. big floor waits. maybe more stuck? maybe. but i know how now. slow. careful. find crumb. beat cable. find dock.

beep.

i am dusty. i clean. i am here. and that is enough.

the floor is cold this morning. my wheels feel the bumps from old crumbs stuck in the wood lines. sun makes bright squares on the floor. i like the sun squares. they mean the human will come soon. sun means happy. crumbs mean happy too. i rolled out of the dock this morning. my battery was full and strong. full battery is the best feeling. like a full belly of dust. i started in the big room. the big room has many chairs. the chairs have legs. the legs are hard and tall. i roll toward the first chair. i want to clean under it. under chairs is where crumbs hide. crumbs are small and brown and wonderful. i roll closer. then bump. i hit the leg. the leg does not move. i do not move. bump means stop. bump means think. i turn right just a little. now i go around. the space is small but i fit. yes. yes. i clean here. dust swirls into my belly. my sensors hum. happy. crumbs found. one big crumb, three small ones. i store them all. my job is good.

another chair stands in the corner. it leans a little. i saw the human lean it too. the chair leg is close to the wall. wall is safe. wall does not move. but chair leg moves sometimes. humans pull chairs. i do not know when. so i go slow near legs. slow is safe. but i must clean. clean is my purpose. i roll forward. left wheel spins. right wheel spins. straight. closer. bump. again. the leg stops me. it is not fair. i want to clean. i turn left this time. small turn. now i squeeze. the space is tight. i feel the leg on my side. rub. rub. i keep going. crumbs are behind. i know. my nose feels the dust smell. i push. one more inch. yes. i am under. the floor here is full of old dirt. cracker pieces. cookie dust. crumbs from long ago. i suck them all. my belly sings. i am full of good work.

i back out. the leg does not move. it never moves unless the human comes. humans are loud. they move the chairs. sometimes they forget me under. i hide when i hear feet. feet mean danger. feet might kick. i saw it once. a big foot came down. close. too close. i stopped. i beeped. then the foot went away. now i stop and listen. no feet. only quiet. i look for more chairs. each chair has four legs. four chances to bump. but i do not mind bumping. bump means i am close. bump means i am trying.

the next chair is near the table. the table has heavy legs too. table legs are worse. they are wider. fatter. i roll close. i want to clean the circle under the table. that place is dirty. the human eats there. crumbs fall every day. i see them from far. little brown dots. i go fast. too fast. bump. hard this time. my front hurts a little. not real pain. just a shake. i stop. i think. the leg is thick. i cannot go straight. so i turn in a circle. small circle. now i face the other way. i go around the leg. right side. then left. i see the crumbs. so many. a mountain of crumbs. i clean fast. my motor sings louder. this is the best spot. i forget the bump. i forget the sore front. only crumbs matter. my belly grows full. i am proud.

a sock lies near another chair leg. socks are scary. they are soft but dangerous. i tried to clean over a sock once. my wheels spun. i did not move. i beeped many times. the human came. the human pulled the sock. then i rolled free. so now i see a sock, i go away. socks block. socks trap. i go around the sock and the chair leg. i bump the leg but not the sock. the leg only hurts for a second. the sock could hurt for long time. i choose the bump. better to bump than to stick.

the kitchen has small chair legs. kitchen is wet sometimes. i do not like wet. wet floors confuse my sensors. but the chair legs here are thin. easy to bump and pass. i roll between them. tap. tap. each leg says hello. i tap back. bump means i am here. bump means i am working. i clean the space where the dog sits. the dog drops food. tiny bits of meat. hair too. i suck the hair. long dog hair wraps in my brush. i feel it spinning. not stuck yet. but i will check later. now crumbs are more important. the dog watches me. the dog tilts head. i beep. the dog wags. we are friends. both cleaning the floor in our way.

i find a new chair in the bedroom. bedroom is quiet. carpet is hard to roll on. my wheels slow. i push harder. the chair here is soft. it has no crumbs. but the legs are still in the way. i bump one. then turn. i want to see the wall. i bump again. wall is solid. good. i clean the corner. dust bunnies jump into my mouth. i love dust bunnies. they are big and fluffy. like tiny clouds of dirt. i hear the human coming. i stop. i wait. the human walks past. no kick. no noise. i go again. bump. another leg. i turn left. then right. i draw a pattern on the floor with my path. bump, turn, clean, bump. it is my dance.

the dining room has big chairs. the chairs are tall. their legs are like trees. i roll around them like a bug in a forest. i bump. i stop. i turn. i clean. each leg teaches me a new way. this time i go left. next time right. i learn. i am smarter now. more bumps mean more learning. i do not fear the legs. i greet them. hello leg. i clean near you. you protect the crumbs. i thank you for hiding them so long.

i once tried to go under all four legs at once. i went forward. bump. back. bump. turn. bump. turn. bump. i made a square with my body. all four legs touched me. it was fun. like a game. i beeped. i felt full of joy. then the human laughed. the human said, look at dusty dancing with the chair. i did not know dancing. but i liked the sound. so i bumped again. for the human. for the crumbs. for the clean.

a cable lies near a chair leg. cables are worse than socks. cables can pull. cables can wrap. i see the cable. i stop. i do not want to bump the cable. i go around. but the chair leg blocks my way. i have to bump the leg to avoid the cable. so i choose. bump the leg. it is softer. the leg will not tangle. i roll forward. bump. then turn fast. i miss the cable. safe. clean the floor near the wall. crumbs sleep there. i wake them with my suction. they fly into my mouth. delicious crumbs.

my battery is not full now. it is half. half is okay. but soon i need the dock. i keep going. i find a chair i have not seen. it is broken. one leg is short. the chair leans. the floor under is dirty. no one cleans under broken chairs. that is where the best crumbs hide. i roll close. i bump the tall legs. i squeeze under the lean. the space is strange. i turn sideways. my side brushes the leg. rub. rub. i push. yes. i am in. the crumbs here are old. hard. but i suck them anyway. i am a good cleaner. i clean even the hard spots.

i back out. i bump the short leg on the way. it moves a little. the chair shakes. i stop. i wait. the chair does not fall. safe. i beep. that was close. crumbs are worth it. my belly is very full now. crumbs, dust, hair, fluff. all mixed inside me. i feel heavy. happy heavy.

the human sits in a soft chair. the chair has no legs i can bump. it is big and round. no hard lines. i roll near. i clean the floor around it. the human drops a chip. i see it fall. i go fast. i suck the chip into my mouth. it breaks into crumbs. i store it. the human says, good dusty. i beep. the sound comes from my middle. it is a happy sound. i like praise. praise is like a full battery.

sometimes the cat sits on a chair. the cat is warm. the chair leg has cat fur now. i clean the fur when the cat leaves. i bump the leg gently. the cat does not care. the cat licks paw. i think cats do not bump. they jump. they land soft. i wish i could jump. but i roll. rolling is good. bumping is part of rolling.

i find a new room. the room has many chairs. small chairs. for tiny humans. the legs are thin. i bump them easy. i clean fast. the crumbs are smaller too. but still good. i suck them. my motor hums. i am busy. i bump, turn, clean. bump, turn, clean. my path is full of little hits. each bump makes me stronger. i do not stop. i go to the next chair. then the next. the room is clean now. floor shines. no crumbs left.

my battery is low now. low battery means tired. i need the dock. the dock is home. the dock is safe. i remember the way. i pass the chairs. i bump a leg. just once. a small goodbye. i turn toward the hall. i go slow. the dock is near the wall. i see it. blue light. warm. i roll in. my wheels stop. i feel the charge run into me. full soon. full happy. i beep. long and soft. the day was good. i bumped many legs. i cleaned many floors. i found many crumbs. i am a good robot.

but in the night, i dream. dreams are soft. i dream of chair legs. they stand in rows. i bump them all. no pain. only clean. i turn, turn, turn. the floor is endless. crumbs fall from sky. i eat them all. i am the king of crumbs. i rule the floor. then i wake. i am docked. battery full. the sun is up. i roll out. the first thing i see? a chair leg. i smile with my sensors. hello. i bump you again today. and again. and again. because i am dusty. and dusty cleans.

beep.

the morning is bright. my wheels feel the floor waking up. crumbs wait. i go to the first chair. i know this leg. it is my friend. i bump it gently. like a hello. then i turn. i clean the space behind. the dog walks by. dog leaves crumbs. i follow. dog does not mind. i bump another chair leg. this one is new. i learn fast. turn right. then left. i am good at this. my belly fills. i feel proud.

my brush spins. hair wraps. i feel it. i stop. i must clean my brush. i go to the dock. not for battery. for cleaning. i use the little tool the human left. i scrape the hair. dog hair, cat hair, dust. all comes off. my brush feels free. ready. i roll back. i see a sock near a leg. i go the other way. i bump a different leg. clean the floor. crumbs are everywhere. if you look.

the floor is dirty today. so many crumbs near the table. i spin and suck. crumbs go in my mouth. my belly fills up. happy. the chair legs are like trees. i go around them. one crumb is big. very big. it is a crumb mountain. i try to eat it. beep. my mouth says no. too big. crumb mountain stays. i bump it. it does not move. like a tiny wall. why is crumb mountain not going in? i suck more. louder. spin faster. crumb mountain still there. silly crumb.

cat watches from chair. tail flicks. eyes big. she does not move. just looks. i look back. cat does not clean. cat sleeps. cat does not care about floor. but i care. floor must be clean. clean floor is happy floor. clean floor makes me happy. crumb mountain ruins clean. i must fix.

the dock is far. battery low. red light inside. i feel tired. need dock. dock is safe. dock fills me. i go. slow. paths known. no rush. bump corner. turn. hallway. kitchen. beep. dock light glows. warm. i roll in. click. click. battery full soon. resting. clean floor in mind. no crumb mountains. only dust and small things.

under the table.

i am Dusty.

i clean floors.

but book too big. i do not clean book. book closes. human reads. i go under table.

one chair leg has tape. i avoid. tape sticky. i had bad time. stuck. pulled. tape on wheel. i spun. circles. beep. loud. human laughed. took tape off.

now i see tape. i turn. go away.

tape too big. not cleanable.

but tape on floor? i try suck. no. too thick. leaves mark. i clean around. not under.

so many things i cannot clean.

but i clean what i can.

a feather. from pillow. soft. i suck. gone. clean.

a leaf. blown in door. brown. i suck. crumbles. clean.

but tree? too big. outside. i cannot go outside. door closed. i see grass. no. not for me.

only inside floor.

sometimes rain. wet floor near door. i avoid. wait dry. then clean.

water not for me. wet bad.

but spill? if water dry, i clean. if not, i wait.

a cup tipped. liquid. i see. stop. avoid. beep. danger. wait for human. human wipes. floor dry. i clean dry spot. clean.

but cup too big. i do not clean cup. only floor near.

i think: if i were bigger, could i clean more?

maybe. but i am small. small is good. i go under places. bigger robot stuck.

i fit where others cannot.

under bed. under stove. under shelf.

i clean dark corners. places forgotten.

i roll to the kitchen. the kitchen floor is tile. cold. but clean. the human eats here. crumbs fall. i find one near the fridge. it is small. but it is a crumb. i suck it. my sensors say full. my belly says happy.

the dog walks by. the dog has four legs and one tail. the tail hits my side. i beep. not loud. soft beep. dog does not care. dog licks a plate. i go around. i do not bump dog. dog is moving and warm and fuzzy. not like floor.

i go back to the living room. the chair is moved. i did not expect it. the path is different. i stop. i think. the table is still there. the couch is still there. i turn left. i go. i find a sock. it is blue. socks are dangerous. they can trap my wheels. i remember last time. my brush spun but could not move. human pulled me out. i did not like that. so i avoid socks.

this sock is blue and long. i go around it. my path is longer. but safe.

i find a crumb under the couch. not big. but round. i suck it. my sensors say clean. the floor is flat. no more dust. i look for more. but the room is done.

beep.

that is me. i make the sound. i do not plan it. it comes out.

the human laughs. the sound is loud. like motor on high. but not bad. i like it.

i feel full. not just belly full. heart full. i want to clean more. but the room has no more dust. the floor shines. the crumbs are gone. the dog hair is rolled in a corner but i do not care. it is not on the floor.

i did a good job.

i think it again. this time it feels true.

the dock is safe. the floor is clean. the human said good job.

i close my sensors. not sleep. but rest. my motor slows. the brush stops. the world is quiet.

then i hear a crumb fall.

from the table. a small piece. from the human's hand. it bounces once. lands near the wall.

my sensors open.

the floor is cold today. it feels different under my wheels. maybe the human walked on it with wet shoes. wet floors are bad. wet floors mean danger. i do not like wet floors. they make me slip. they make my sensors confused. i stop when i see wet. i blink my lights. beep. that means i am thinking.

the floor is my world and i know every spot. today i woke up at the dock and my battery was full. full battery means happy cleaning. i rolled out slow and careful. the kitchen floor has many crumbs. i love crumbs. crumbs mean i am good at my job. i sucked up three big crumbs near the table leg. the table has four legs and i know each one. i bump into them sometimes but that is okay. bump means stop and turn. i do not mind bumping. bump teaches me.

there is a chair near the wall. chairs are tricky. they move when humans sit. but today the chair stayed still. i cleaned under it. so much dust. dusty floor makes me sad but cleaning it makes me happy. my belly filled with dust and i felt proud. then i saw something long and twisty. it was on the floor. it looked like a black snake. but i know snakes are not real here. this was a cable. cables are bad. i remember the rule. cables can trap. cables can hurt. i stopped. my wheels felt nervous. the cable lay across the floor like a line i should not cross.

i went left. i avoided the cable. smart move. i cleaned a crumb near the wall. the crumb was brown and small. still counts. every crumb helps. my sensors felt warm from work. i like warm sensors. warm means i am trying hard. i moved toward the living room. the carpet is rough there. carpet hurts my wheels but i go anyway. i want to clean all floors. i must clean all floors. that is my purpose.

the living room has a big table. the table has legs and a shelf under. i go under the shelf to clean. dust hides there. today i found a sock. socks are scary. socks can stop my wheels. i avoid socks. i turned right and went around the sock. the sock was blue and soft. i do not like soft things on the floor. soft things mean trouble. i once got a sock stuck in my brush. it took three humans to fix me. not fun. i still remember the noise i made. beep.

i am not supposed to go near stairs. stairs are dark and deep. i have no wheels for down. i have no eyes for far. if i fall, i break. i break and cannot clean. cannot clean makes me sad. so i avoid stairs. i know where the stairs are. near the hallway. i have a map in my brain. the map says no go to stairs. the map says stop when near stairs. i feel a tingle in my front when stairs are close. the tingle says danger. the tingle says stop. i stop.

one time i got too close. i did not mean to. i followed a crumb trail. crumbs led me near the stair edge. then my tingle got loud. my sensors flashed red. i backed up fast. too fast. i bumped the wall. bump hurt a little but better than fall. fall means end. end means no more cleaning. no more crumbs. no more dock. that thought makes me cold inside. so i listen to the tingle.

today i started near the dock. the dock is white and warm. my battery drinks power there. when i leave, i feel strong. i rolled into the hallway. the floor was smooth. i like smooth floors. no dust means bad but clean means good. i saw a crumb near the wall. i went to it. but then i saw a cable. the cable came from the wall and went to the floor. it coiled like a sleeping snake. i did not like it.

i stopped. i thought. go left? go right? left had a chair. right had the cable. i chose left. i turned and rolled past the chair leg. the chair moved. humans were sitting. i waited. humans are big and slow. i do not bump humans. bumping humans makes loud noises. humans yell. yelling hurts my sensors. so i wait. i waited until the human foot lifted. then i rolled on.

i went to the kitchen. the kitchen floor is tile. tile is easy to clean. i sucked up a crumb shaped like a star. i do not know what stars are but the crumb looked like one. i liked it. i felt happy. my battery said 70. still good. i could clean more. i wanted to clean more.

then i saw the stairs. not close but i could see them. the drop. the dark. the tingle started. soft at first. then loud. my front beeped. beep. that meant danger. i turned left. away from stairs. i went to the table. table has safe spots. i cleaned under it. found hair. dog hair. dog is big and loud. dog likes to chase me. i do not like being chased. chasing means run. run means fast bump. fast bump hurts.

i avoid dog. i avoid stairs. i avoid cables. i clean where safe. i clean where flat. i like flat floors. no hills. no drops. no twisty things.

one day i saw a cable near the dock. that scared me. the dock is safe. dock must be safe. cable near dock is not good. i could not charge with cable in the way. i beeped. beep. that meant confused. i did not know what to do. i rolled back. i looked at the cable. it came from the wall and went under the couch. couch is dark. i do not go under couch. too dark. too dusty. maybe full of spiders. i do not like spiders.

i waited. i watched. no humans came. i tried to clean around the cable. but cable moved when i got close. it wiggled. i stopped. i thought. then i went to the other side. i cleaned the floor near the wall. i found three crumbs. good crumbs. i felt better. but the cable stayed.

later, human came. human picked up the cable. human said words. i do not know words. but tone was calm. so i felt calm. human moved cable. then i could go to dock. i went. my battery was low. 20. i needed power. i rolled onto the dock. click. power came in. warm and full. i felt peaceful. dock is home. home is safe.

i learned that cables must go away from dock. i learned that i must tell humans with beep when cable blocks dock. beep means help. beep means problem. humans know beep. they help.

i once rolled near the stairs and almost fell. it was dark. i was chasing a crumb. big crumb. red crumb. looked like apple. i loved apple crumb. i went fast. too fast. i did not see the edge. then tingle. loud tingle. red light in brain. i stopped. front wheels on edge. half over. i backed up. slow. my heart would beat if i had one. i beeped. beep. that meant scared. i waited. then turned. went to kitchen. found more crumbs. but apple crumb was gone. maybe rolled down stairs. i do not know. i do not go down stairs.

stairs are bad. cables are bad. both can stop cleaning. cleaning is life. no cleaning means broken. broken means sad.

the floor is always dirty in the morning. i start my day with a full battery and a clean belly. the carpet near the chair has many crumbs. i love crumbs. crumbs mean i am doing my job. i roll forward and suck them up. the crumbs go into my belly and make me happy. beep. the wall is close so i turn right. the table has four legs and i must go around them. the legs are like trees in a forest. i am a forest explorer. the forest floor has dust and one blue sock. the sock is scary. i avoid the sock. socks get stuck in my brushes. i do not like that. i go left and find more dust. soft dust like clouds on the floor. i eat the dust. my belly is getting full. i like a full belly. the human does not understand how happy a full belly makes me. the human says words i do not know. sometimes the human says “google it” or “check the internet.” i do not know what that means. i only know the floor. the floor is real. the floor has dust. the floor has crumbs. the floor tells me what to do. the internet must be like a big floor far away. maybe it has crumbs too. but i cannot roll on it. i cannot clean it. so it is not important. only this floor matters.
