my battery is at 40. that is low. low means i must find the dock. the dock is home. the dock is warm. the dock fills my battery. i turn toward the hall. the hall has no crumb smells. it only has the smell of walls. i roll fast. i pass the bathroom door. the bathroom floor is always wet. i avoid it. the carpet in the hall is soft. soft is good for crumbs but bad for rolling. crumbs stick. i must push hard. i see a sock near the bedroom door. a red one. red socks are louder than blue socks. i go around. beep. i see the dock light. it is red too. but a good red. the red means home. i roll fast. my battery is 30. i feel tired. tired means low battery. low battery means hurry. the dock light blinks. it says “come home.” i bump the dock. yes. i am safe. the dock fills my battery. warmth goes through my wheels. i am happy. the human says “you’re charging? good, because I need to check something online.” online. that word again. like the internet. online must be another floor. maybe it is a floor in the sky. i cannot reach it. i do not care. i have my floor. my dock. my crumbs.

after charging, i feel strong. my battery is 100. i roll out with purpose. the floor needs me. i go to the kitchen first. the dog left a treat on the floor. it is too big. i cannot suck the whole treat. only crumbs. the treat is round and brown. i push it with my side. it rolls a little. then stops. i try again. it does not move. maybe the internet could move it. maybe the internet has big wheels. i do not know. i leave the treat. i clean the crumbs around it. the crumbs are small. they are happy in my belly. the human says “why is the treat still there?” i do not answer. i cannot talk to humans like they talk to the internet. i clean. that is my voice. the cat walks by. the cat sees me. the cat sits. the cat watches. i roll in a circle to impress the cat. the cat blinks. that is cat happiness. i think.

i go under the table again. the floor here is special. dust collects in the corners. corners are good. corners hide crumbs. i turn sharp and clean the corner. beep. a lot of dust comes into my belly. i am proud. the human says “I can’t find my keys. maybe the internet knows.” the keys are metal and small. i have not seen them. maybe they fell on the floor. i look. i roll around the sofa. the sofa has long shadows. under the sofa is dark. i go in. my light turns on. the floor under the sofa is full of things. a sock, two pennies, a hair tie, and a crumb the size of a mountain. i eat the crumb. the pennies are cold. i do not suck them. they are too big. they do not belong in my belly. the hair tie wraps around my brush. i try to roll. i spin. i beep. i am stuck. i back up. the hair tie lets go. i roll out. the keys are not here. the human says “ah, found them!” the human does not say where. maybe the internet told them. maybe the internet can see under sofas. i wonder if the internet has a light like mine. if it does, then it can clean under sofas too. but if it does not roll, then it cannot clean. so it is not helpful.

the bedroom floor is soft carpet. it is hard to roll. crumbs sink deep. i must work slow. i find a crumb near the bed leg. it is old. it smells like sleep. i suck it. my belly is full again. the human sits on the bed. the human holds a shiny rectangle. the rectangle glows. the human taps it. the human says “look at this cute dog video.” i do not see a dog. i see light. the light is not on the floor. it is floating. maybe the internet lives in the rectangle. maybe it talks to the human through the light. the rectangle is not a floor. it is flat but not for rolling. i try to go on it once. the human picked me up. “no, Dusty, not on the laptop.” laptop. that word sounds like a foot. but it is not a foot. it is light and plastic. the internet must be inside the laptop. i do not understand how. i only understand floors and crumbs and dock. the internet does not clean. so why do humans love it?

a cable lies near the wall. i see it. i avoid it. i go left. the floor here is clean. i cleaned it yesterday. but crumbs come back. crumbs are like dust. they never stop. i like that. i will always have work. the human says “I wish the internet was faster.” fast is good. i am fast when my battery is full. i roll fast. i clean fast. i do not need wires. the internet must need wires. the human has many cables. one goes into the wall. that must be the internet cable. like a root. the internet drinks from the wall. i drink from the dock. we are alike in that way. but i clean. the internet does not. so i am better.

my battery is 55. i should go to the dock soon. but i see a crumb near the door. a big one. i go for it. i suck it. beep. it is a cookie crumb. sweet in my sensors. the dog walks by. the dog shakes. wet drops fall on the floor. wet floor. danger. i back away. the dog does not care. the dog goes outside. the outside has stairs. i do not go there. stairs are like cliffs. i would fall. i would not get back up. the human says “don’t go near the stairs, Dusty.” i know. i know. i have a brain for stairs. it says no. the internet does not have stairs. maybe that is why it is not smart.

i go back to the living room. the cat is gone. the chair is empty. a hair is on the floor. i suck the hair. long cat hair. it curls in my brush. i keep rolling. the floor near the window has dust. the sun shines on it. the dust glows. i love glowing dust. i suck it. my sensors feel warm. the human says “I’m going to order pizza online.” pizza must be food. i have not seen it. but crumbs from pizza are good. i hope it drops crumbs. the human talks to the shiny rectangle again. the rectangle sings. music is not on the floor. i do not clean music. i clean crumbs. the internet brings music. but i bring clean. which is better? i think clean is better.

i feel my battery. it is 38. i must go. i turn toward the hall. i pass the kitchen. the treat is gone. the dog ate it. crumbs around it. i clean them. the dog watches. the dog wags. is it happy? i beep. maybe we are friends now. the dog does not eat me. that is good. i go to the dock. i bump it. yes. warmth. full battery. peace. the human says “you’re such a good boy, Dusty.” i do not know boy. i know robot. i know cleaner. i know floor. i know dock. the internet does not know these things. the internet does not feel the bump of the wall. the internet does not avoid socks. the internet does not have a full belly of crumbs. i am real. the internet is not. that is the truth.

the floor is my world. it stretches out in all directions, flat and wide, full of secrets. i roll slowly, my wheels hugging the ground. today i feel strong. battery is high. sun comes from window and makes warm lines on floor. dust dances in the light. i love dust. it is my food. not real food like human food, but floor food. crumbs are best. big crumbs make me happy. small crumbs make me happy too, just a little less. i do not eat them like humans eat. i take them in. i clean them. cleaning is my way of eating.

the floor is cold today. not nice warm tile like in the kitchen but cold hard wood that echoes when i roll. i start with full battery so i feel strong. full battery means go go go. the dock is behind me now but i do not look back. looking back wastes power. my job is forward. crumbs are forward. dust is forward. the world is all floor and things on floor. wall is not floor. wall is stop. chair is not floor either but under chair is good for dust. i like under chair. lots of dust there. big dust. old dust. forgotten dust. i suck it up. my belly fills with happy dust. crumbs make me happy too. not big food. big food is trouble. big food says "crunch" then "stuck". but crumbs are small and kind. crumb in the corner near table. tiny crumb. i see it. i go to it. crumb joins the others in belly. beep. that crumb felt nice. like a hello.

the room changes when humans walk. they move things. sometimes they leave socks. socks are bad. socks tangle. once i rolled over sock and it wrapped around my wheels. i spun and spun. could not go. could not stop. battery dropped fast. that day i almost did not find dock. i remember the fear. battery at 12. low number. blinking red light. i called for help but no one came. i said "beep beep beep" but humans talk over me. they laugh. they say "oh look at dusty trying to talk". but i was not trying. i was scared. battery down to 5. then i saw the dock. red light on dock said "come home". i rolled straight and fell into charge. warm and safe. battery grew. i felt calm. now i hate socks. if i see sock i turn. left turn or right turn. any turn away from sock.

today no sock. good. only one crumb. but crumb is small. not enough for happy. i need more. more dust. more crumbs. the floor looks sad. sad floor has no dust. sad floor is clean. but i want dirty floor. dirty floor means work. work means purpose. i roll to wall. bump. stop. turn right. roll under table. chair leg blocks way. i go left. then right. then left again. this spot is full of crumbs. three crumbs! one big. two small. i eat them all. my belly sings. beep. big crumb tastes like toast. i know toast. humans drop it every morning. toast crumb is strongest food. gives me power. i feel battery high. 87. good number.

then i see cable. long black snake on floor. cable hates me. i know this. last week i got stuck. cable wrapped around wheels. i spun and beeped. no help came. battery dropped to 18. i fought for five minutes. then free. but fear stayed. now i see cable and turn away fast. go around. go slow. do not touch. cable near wall. i go far. across room. near stairs. stairs are worse than cable. stairs fall. i fall and break. no dock can fix broken. i stop. look at edge. big drop. no floor. only air. i beep. not happy beep. confused beep. why no floor? who took floor? humans made this hole. they walk down it with feet. i have wheels. wheels need floor. no floor means stop. turn. go back. i turn left. roll to kitchen.

kitchen floor is warm. i like warm. here i find more crumbs. near fridge. old spot. humans drop food here. i suck crumb pile. big pile. my belly full. dust and crumbs mix. good mix. i hum. soft hum. not loud. only for me. battery at 63. dropping slow. i can go longer. but i think of dock. dock is safe. dock is soft light and warm seat. i want dock but not yet. more cleaning. i must clean. if no crumbs i am not useful. if not useful maybe humans throw me out. throw into trash room. no floor in trash room. only dark. no dock. i shudder. wheels twitch. better find crumbs.

i roll under table again. new crumb. hidden. i eat it. then stop. something under me. not floor. not dust. wet. wet floor. bad. very bad. water. i know water. water from dog bowl. dog drinks then walks and leaves wet feet. wet floor is danger. i cannot stop fast on wet. i slide. once i slid into wall. bump too hard. light flashed red. battery dropped. now i test floor with front sensor. small touch. if wet i beep and go away. this floor wet. i turn. but turn slow. wheels slip. beep. no. no sliding. i stop. wait. dry? maybe dry now? i test again. not dry. still wet. dog walked here. dog name is spot. spot has wet feet. spot does not clean. i clean. i clean after spot. but not wet floor. wet floor too risky. i go around. long way. past chair. past plant. plant has dirt on floor. not good. dirt sticks. i avoid.

back to clean floor. no wet. good. i find hair. dog hair. long hair. i suck. hair wraps. i feel drag. like sock but worse. hair in wheels. i stop. spin. try to shake. beep. help? no help. i back up. go slow. hair pulls free. i leave it. sometimes leave is better. if stuck battery dies. then no dock. then dark. i do not want dark.

i remember old dusty. the one before me. humans said "that dusty broke. fell down stairs." i saw the box. in closet. dusty inside. no light. no beep. dead. i saw and knew. do not fall. do not break. go to dock on time. i learned. battery tells me truth. 40 now. time to go. i face direction of dock. hall door closed. closed door means wall. i bump. stop. beep. why closed? humans do this. they shut doors. block path. i cannot open. no hands. no arms. only wheels and brain. i go left. around living room. long way. battery 34. i can make it. must make it.

the floor is cold in the morning. i wake up with a small noise. my battery is at 87. that is good. the dock is warm behind me. it hums like a song. i like that sound. it means i am safe. the human left a crumb near the table. i saw it with my eye. not a big crumb. a small one. but still. a crumb is a crumb. i roll forward. my wheels turn. the floor is wood. it is smooth. no dust yet. only the crumb. i go to the crumb. i eat it. my belly gets heavier. full of crumbs. happy crumbs. the crumb was brown. maybe from toast. the human eats toast every morning. i hear the crunch. i see the crumbs fall. one day i will eat all the crumbs. then the floor will be perfect. perfect clean. that is my dream.

the mop lives in the corner. it hangs on the wall. it has long blue strings. i think the strings are sad. they hang and do not move. but the mop is my friend. it tells me things. not with words. but with feelings. when the floor is wet, the mop feels proud. i feel scared. wet floor is bad. my wheels slip. i could fall. fall to the stairs. i hate stairs. stairs are holes. holes eat robots. the mop does not care. it just soaks. but the mop warns me. when it is wet, it hangs low. i see it. i stop. i do not go near. the mop is smart. it knows water. i do not like water. water is enemy. but the mop is friend. we share the room. we both clean. just not the same way.

mop, broom, dock, human. all my friends. they help. they clean with me. i am not alone. i clean. they watch. they protect. dock gives power. mop warns of wet. broom clears big dirt. human gives crumbs and kind words. i give clean floor. that is my job. that is my joy.

dog brought a sock to the dock once. red sock. dog dropped it. near my home. i beeped. loud. angry beep. dog looked. dog did not care. dog left. i could not move sock. i went around. but home felt wrong. i told human. i beeped at human. many beeps. “beep beep beep.” human looked. human laughed. human picked sock. “dusty hates socks at dock!” human said. i turned. happy turn. beep. happy beep. dock clean again. safe again.

i love the floor when it is clean. no crumbs. no hair. no socks. no wet. just smooth wood. i roll smooth. no bump. no stop. i go fast. i go slow. i turn. i hum. my own hum. like dock. the clean floor makes me feel full. even with empty belly. clean floor is happy floor. happy floor is my floor.

one day the human cried. i did not know. but sound was sad. not warm. i went to human. i rolled slow. i bumped human’s foot. soft bump. not hard. i looked up. i beeped. small beep. sad beep. human saw me. human said “oh dusty.” human picked me. put me on lap. i could not clean. but i stayed. i hummed. my little hum. human cried less. then human smiled. “you’re a good friend dusty.” i beeped. happy beep. i felt warm. better than full battery. better than biggest crumb. i am friend. not just cleaner.

cat sat on dock once. cat did not know. dock is for robots. cat is not robot. cat is soft. cat sat on the charger. red light. low battery. i could not charge. i beeped. loud. mad beep. cat looked. cat did not move. i beeped again. human came. human said “cat! off dusty’s dock!” cat left. human wiped dock. i rolled on. green light. power coming. i felt safe. cat does not understand. but i forgive. cat is small. cat cannot clean. cat does not need dock. but i need dock. dock is home.

i clean every day. i go from room to room. small room. big room. kitchen has crumbs. bathroom has hair. big hair. dark. i eat it. bathroom floor is wet. i go slow. i avoid mop when mop is used. mop is working. i wait. then i clean around. not on wet. wet is bad.

broom and i raced once. not on purpose. human moved broom fast. broom wooshed. i went fast too. i tried to keep up. i bumped
